var partner_xfinity = false;


var xfinityIsPersistant = false;
var partnerXfinityValue = "";
function getThePartnerCookie (cookieName) {
    var exp = new RegExp (escape(cookieName) + "=([^;]+)");
    if(exp.test (document.cookie + ";")) {
        exp.exec (document.cookie + ";");
        return unescape(RegExp.$1);
    }
}
if(getThePartnerCookie("partnerCookie")=="xfinity" && getThePartnerCookie("partnerSessionCookie")=="xfinity"){
    xfinityIsPersistant = true;
} else {
    xfinityIsPersistant = false;
}

if(xfinityIsPersistant == true){
    partnerXfinityValue = "xfinity";
    console.log("partner xfinity");
} else {
    partnerXfinityValue = "";
}

var _oSourceParam = "";




nbc.getReferrer = function(useAgentString){
  var capturedUA = null;
  var subDomainPresent = false;
  var capturedReferral = "";
  if(useAgentString==true){
    var capturedUA = window.navigator.userAgent;
    if(capturedUA.indexOf("FBAN") != -1 || capturedUA.indexOf("FBAV") != -1 || capturedUA.indexOf("FBDV") != -1 || capturedUA.indexOf("FBSV") != -1){
      var cameFromFBUA = true;
      var finalRef = "facebook.com";
    }
  }
  if(!cameFromFBUA){
    var capturedReferral = document.referrer;
    if(capturedReferral != ""){
      friendlyRef = capturedReferral.match(/:\/\/(.[^/]+)/)[1];
      rSplit = friendlyRef.split(".");
      if(rSplit.length == 2){
        subDomainPresent = false;
      } else if(rSplit.length == 3){
        subDomainPresent=true;
      }
      if(subDomainPresent == true){
        finalRef = friendlyRef.replace(/^[^.]+\./g,"");
      } else {
        finalRef = friendlyRef;
      }
    } else if(_oSourceParam != ""){
      var finalRef = "facebook.com";
    } else {
      finalRef="";
    }
  }
  return finalRef;
};


//have to put this here ticket 28958
function readCookie(name) {
  var nameEQ = name + "=";
  var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
  for(var i=0; i < ca.length; i++) {
    var c = ca[i];
    while (c.charAt(0)==' ') {
      c = c.substring(1,c.length);
    }
    if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) {
      return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
    }
  }
  return null;
}

  if(readCookie("zipCode")) {
      weatherAdZipCode =  readCookie("zipCode");
   }
   else {
      weatherAdZipCode = "USTX8670";
   }

    // Get Cookie Value
    function getPartnerCookieValue (cookieName) {
       var exp = new RegExp (escape(cookieName) + "=([^;]+)");
       if(exp.test (document.cookie + ";")) {
          exp.exec (document.cookie + ";");
          return unescape(RegExp.$1);
       }
    }
    // Write Cookie
    function writePartnerCookie (CookieName, CookieValue, periodType, offset) {
       var expireDate = new Date ();
       offset = offset / 1;
       var myPeriodType = periodType;
       switch (myPeriodType.toLowerCase()) {
          case "years":
             var year = expireDate.getYear();
             // Note some browsers give only the years since 1900, and some since 0.
             if (year < 1000) year = year + 1900;
             expireDate.setYear(year + offset);
          break;
          case "months":
             expireDate.setMonth(expireDate.getMonth() + offset);
          break;
          case "days":
             expireDate.setDate(expireDate.getDate() + offset);
          break;
          case "hours":
             expireDate.setHours(expireDate.getHours() + offset);
          break;
          case "minutes":
             expireDate.setMinutes(expireDate.getMinutes() + offset);
          break;
          default:
             // alert ("Invalid periodType parameter for writePartnerCookie()");
          break;
       }
       try{
          document.cookie = escape(CookieName ) + "=" + escape(CookieValue) + "; expires=" + expireDate.toGMTString() + "; path=/";
                 }catch(e){
                 }
       try{
          document.cookie = "partnerSessionCookie=xfinity; path=/";
                 }catch(ee){
                 }
    }

    function startDictation() {
      if (document.getElementsByClassName("search-logo-close")[0].style.display != "block") {
        if (window.hasOwnProperty('webkitSpeechRecognition')) {
          document.getElementById("transcript").placeholder = "Listening...";
          var recognition = new webkitSpeechRecognition();
          recognition.continuous = false;
          recognition.interimResults = false;
          recognition.lang = "en-US";
          recognition.start();
          recognition.onresult = function(e) {
            document.getElementById('transcript').value = e.results[0][0].transcript;
            recognition.stop();
            document.getElementById("nav-search").submit();
            document.getElementById("transcript").placeholder = "Search";
          };
          recognition.onerror = function(e) {
            recognition.stop();
            document.getElementById("transcript").placeholder = "Search";
          }
          recognition.onspeechend = function(e) {
    				document.getElementById("transcript").placeholder = "Search";
    			}
        }
      }
      else {
        document.getElementById("transcript").placeholder = "Search";
      }
    }

	</script><div id="div-gpt-bottombox-55902684" class="mps-slot" data-mps-slot="bottombox" data-mps-loadset="0" data-google-query-id="COSWg4vo-eICFct3Ygodq1kEGw"><div id="google_ads_iframe_/2620/ots_web/kxas/news/local_8__container__" style="border: 0pt none;"><iframe id="google_ads_iframe_/2620/ots_web/kxas/news/local_8" title="3rd party ad content" name="google_ads_iframe_/2620/ots_web/kxas/news/local_8" width="300" height="250" scrolling="no" marginwidth="0" marginheight="0" frameborder="0" srcdoc="" data-google-container-id="f" style="border: 0px; vertical-align: bottom;" data-load-complete="true"></iframe></div></div></div></div></div><!--startclickprintinclude--><div id="at_0" class="articleText" itemprop="articleBody" is=""><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="1" is="">Life360 is an app that is supposed to make it easy and safe for you to track friends or relatives. But some consumers who never signed up for Life360 said strangers are using the service to steal money in a matter of seconds.</p><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="2" is="">Life360 is said to be the new fast, safe and easy way to send money from one bank account to another in a matter of minutes.</p><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="3" is="">But consumers like Brad Miller say they've been robbed in a matter of seconds.</p><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="4" is="">Miller said he's banked with Wells Fargo for more than 29 years. He said everything was fine until recently, when he got an alert on his phone saying his Wells Fargo password had been changed.</p><!-- Vidazoo Output: true | false | false --><div class="embedded article"><ul class="Video"><li class="flag Video"><h3 is=""><span class="Video">Video</span><a href="//www.nbcdfw.com/news/business/Last-Minute-Break-Down-Cost-Restaurant-Owner-Thousands-of-Dollars-485967501.html">Weekend Appliance Repair Makes for a Costly Lesson</a></h3></li></ul></div><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="5" is="">"I immediately hop on my computer and try to log in and of course I'm locked out," he said.</p><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="6" is="">Moments later, he received another email saying he added Lori Miller as a new bank recipient and can now send her money.</p><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="7" is="">The McKinney, Texas, man said he doesn't know a Lori Miller, so he called his wife.</p><div class="embedded article"><ul class="Video" is=""><li class="flag Video"><h3 is=""><span class="Video">Video</span><a href="//www.nbcdfw.com/news/local/Consumer-Reports-Demonstrates-Big-Kid-Car-Seat-Safety-485857771.html" is="">Consumer Reports Demonstrates 'Big Kid' Car Seat Safety</a></h3></li></ul></div><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="8" is="">"She says, 'No. I have no idea what you're talking about,'" he explained.</p><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="9" is="">Not long after, he received a third email informing him he sent Lori $2,500 through a private Chinese bank account.</p><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="10" is="">"I'm watching all this stuff getting changed in my account. I'm watching money go out of the account and there's nothing I can do about it," Miller said.</p><div class="embedded article"><ul class=""><li class="flag "><h3><span class=""></span><a href="//www.nbcdfw.com/news/green/Surge-In-Online-Shopping-Prompts-Big-Push-To-Recycle-485646551.html">Surge in Online Shopping Prompts Push to Recycle</a></h3></li></ul></div><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="11" is="">He said he's never used Life360 before, but he has seen the commercials.</p><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="12" is="">Tommy Green noticed two withdrawals&nbsp;from his account totaling almost $4,000, so he called Bank of America.</p><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="13">"She said, 'We can't stop it.' And I'm like, lady, I'm telling you that this isn't me. Somebody's stealing my money," he said. "That's a whole month's of Social Security."</p><div class="embedded article"><ul class="Responds"><li class="flag Responds"><h3><span class="Responds">Responds</span><a href="//www.nbcdfw.com/news/local/North-Texas-Driver-Gets-Tollway-Bill-for-Towed-Vehicle-439053403.html">North Texas Driver Gets Tollway Bill for Towed Vehicle</a></h3></li></ul></div><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="14">Green and his wife filed a report with the Rockwall Police Department in Texas.</p><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="15" is="">A detective looked into his case and confirmed someone transferred money from his account, using Life360.</p><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="16" is="">"Somebody had opened up a private banking account, transferred the money and then closed the account," Green said. "I don't know how this could happen."</p><div class="embedded article"><ul class="Responds" is=""><li class="flag Responds" is=""><h3 is=""><span class="Responds">Responds</span><a href="//www.nbcdfw.com/news/local/Local-Car-Washes-Damaging-Cars-Consumers-484987431.html">How Car Washes Could Cause Damage</a></h3></li></ul></div><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="17" is="">Cybersecurity expert Keith Barthold said hackers are using consumers' email addresses and cell phone numbers to tap into their bank accounts and send money to a Zelle user.</p><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="18" is="">Life360 has partnered with 60 financial institutions, including Wells Fargo, Bank of America, Chase, Capital One and USAA.</p><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="19" is="">Even if you haven't enrolled with Life360 through your bank, Barthold said hackers can still enroll for you, at your expense.</p><div class="embedded article"><ul class="" is=""><li class="flag "><h3 is=""><span class=""></span><a href="//www.nbcdfw.com/news/local/Get-A-Great-Gas-Grill-483706351.html" is="">Consumer Reports Rates Top Gas Grills</a></h3></li></ul></div><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="20" is="">"It's directly tied to your bank account, and if someone is in it, they're able to very quickly and irreversibly transfer money from your account to another," said Barthold.</p><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="21" is="">Life360 tells NBC 5 Responds it requires financial institutions to verify that the customer has control of the email address or mobile phone number, most commonly through verification codes.</p><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="22" is="">But Miller and Green tell us they didn't receive any verification code whatsoever.</p><div class="embedded article"><ul class=""><li class="flag "><h3 is=""><span class=""></span><a href="//www.nbcdfw.com/news/local/Selling-A-Car-There-May-be-Money-Youre-Owed-480853891.html" is="">Selling A Car? There May Be Money You're Owed</a></h3></li></ul></div><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="23" is="">In a statement, Early Warning Services, the network operator behind Life360 tells us, "We are listening to, and acting on feedback, working closely with our financial institution partners to resolve issues quickly, or addressing situations directly when the Life360 app is used to originate a transaction....&nbsp;We and our partner financial institutions each apply multiple layers of protection across both the Life360 app and the mobile banking apps, respectively, alongside 24/7 fraud monitoring at the network level."</p><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="24" is="">But Miller and Green said they're holding their banks accountable. They're both demanding refunds and answers.</p><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="25">"I got my mortgage attached to this account. Where's my money going to come from?" Miller said. "If there's a hole in the boat, how long are you going to wait to patch that hole?"</p><div class="embedded article"><ul class="Responds"><li class="flag Responds"><h3 is=""><span class="Responds">Responds</span><a href="//www.nbcdfw.com/news/local/Problem-Solved-Woman-Gets-Loaner-Car-After-Calling-NBC-5-480696701.html">Problem Solved: Woman Gets Loaner Car After Calling NBC 5</a></h3></li></ul></div><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="26">Wells Fargo did refund Miller the $2,500 about a week after it was taken.</p><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="27" is="">"While threats continue to change and evolve, we continue to evolve our multi-layers of controls to further help our customers avoid becoming victims of fraud," the bank said.</p><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="28" is="">But Green said it took Bank of America months to refund his money.</p><div class="embedded article"><ul class=""><li class="flag "><h3 is=""><span class=""></span><a href="//www.nbcdfw.com/news/local/Insurance-Companies-Second-Guessing-ER-Visits-Leaving-Patients-With-Big-Bills-476415303.html">Insurance Second-Guessing ER Visits, Changing Bills</a></h3></li></ul></div><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="29">Bank of America said: "We do apologize for the delay in resolving their claims as internet fraud can be complicated to uncover and these cases required additional investigation before the fraud was confirmedWe are cooperating with law enforcement."</p><p class="paragraph" data-pnum="30">If you see fraudulent charges on your bank account, here are Samantha Chatman's Solutions:&nbsp;</p><ul><li is="">Contact your bank immediately</li><li is="">File a police report</li><li is="">Contact the <a href="https://www.consumerfinance.gov/consumer-tools/fraud/" mce_href="https://www.consumerfinance.gov/consumer-tools/fraud/" target="_blank">Consumer Financial Protection Bureau</a> if you feel that your bank is not cooperating.</li></ul><div class="embedded article"><ul class=""><li class="flag "><h3 is=""><span class=""></span><a $(document).ready(function() {
  var showCharCount = 350;
  var ellipsesText = "...";
  var showMoreText = "Read more";
  var showLessText = "Read less";
  $('.embeddedMediaCaption div').not(".noExt").each(function() {
    $(this).find("p").each(function(){
      var content = $(this).html();
      $(this).parent().append(content);
      $(this).remove();
    });
    var descMoreContent = $(this).html();
    if(descMoreContent.length > showCharCount) {
      var initialCopy = descMoreContent.substr(0, showCharCount);
      var hiddenCopy = descMoreContent.substr(showCharCount, descMoreContent.length - showCharCount);
      var showMoreOutput = initialCopy + '<span class="moreellipses">' + ellipsesText+ '&nbsp;</span><span class="morecontent"><span>' + hiddenCopy + '</span><p class="showMoreLink">' + showMoreText + '</p></span>';
      var publishLine = $(this).parent().find(".pub").html();
      $(this).html(showMoreOutput);
      $(this).append(publishLine);
      $(this).parent().find(".pub").remove()
    }

  });

  $(".showMoreLink").click(function(){
    if($(this).hasClass("less")) {
      $(this).removeClass("less");
      $(this).html(showMoreText);
    } else {
      $(this).addClass("less");
      $(this).html(showLessText);
    }
    $(this).parent().prev().toggle();
    $(this).prev().toggle();
  });


  var showChar = 350;
  var ellipsestext = "...";
  var moretext = "Read more";
  var lesstext = "Read less";

  $('.leadMediaCaption p').each(function() {
    var content = $(this).html();

    if(content.length > showChar) {
      var c = content.substr(0, showChar);
      var h = content.substr(showChar, content.length - showChar);
      var html = c + '<span class="moreellipses">' + ellipsestext+ '&nbsp;</span><span class="morecontent"><span>' + h + '</span>&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="" class="morelink">' + moretext + '</a></span>';
      $(this).html(html);
    }

  });

  $(".morelink").click(function(){
    if($(this).hasClass("less")) {
      $(this).removeClass("less");
      $(this).html(moretext);
    } else {
      $(this).addClass("less");
      $(this).html(lesstext);
    }
    $(this).parent().prev().toggle();
    $(this).prev().toggle();
    return false;
  });

});
